The room is very clean, the bathroom is relatively large, and the facilities are relatively old-school decoration, but the sound insulation is good, the view is good, and the air conditioning is powerful. These are enough.
Breakfast costs 108 per person, with rich varieties and good value for money. There are all kinds of Chinese and Western styles, but there are a few bakery products. There are no cakes, only buns and toast.
